 \"text\": \"# Chromium Blink Rendering Pipeline: Style to Paint\\n\\n## Pipeline Stages\\n\\nThis trace follows how CSS style changes propagate through Chromium's Blink rendering engine across five critical stages:\\n\\n### 1. Style Resolution\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/style_resolver.h`\\n**Class:** `StyleResolver` (line 63)\\n\\nThe `StyleResolver` class is the starting point of the rendering pipeline. It resolves computed styles for DOM elements based on the document's collection of stylesheets (user styles, author styles, UA styles). There is a 1-1 relationship between `StyleResolver` and `Document`. The `ResolveStyle` method produces a `ComputedStyle` for each element.\\n\\n### 2. Layout Tree Generation\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/layout_object.h`\\n**Class:** `LayoutObject` (line 270)\\n\\nThe `LayoutObject` class is the base class for the layout tree. It represents the layout abstraction of a DOM node. Layout objects are created based on the computed styles from `StyleResolver`. Each `LayoutObject` inherits from `GarbageCollected<LayoutObject>`, `ImageResourceObserver`, and `DisplayItemClient`, connecting the layout tree to the painting system.\\n\\n### 3. Painting Layer Hierarchy\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/paint_layer.h`\\n**Class:** `PaintLayer` (line 174)\\n\\nThe `PaintLayer` class represents the painting layer abstraction. Not all `LayoutObject` instances have a corresponding `PaintLayer`—only those that establish a stacking context or have special painting requirements. `PaintLayer` objects form a tree that determines the order and grouping of painting operations. Each `PaintLayer` maintains a reference to its associated `LayoutBoxModelObject`.\\n\\n### 4. Paint Controller and Display Item Processing\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h`\\n**Class:** `PaintController` (line 131)\\n\\nThe `PaintController` is responsible for processing display items as they are produced during the painting traversal, and producing a final paint artifact when complete. It manages caching, cache invalidation, and merging of paint operations. During the paint walk, painters append display items to the `PaintController`'s display item list.\\n\\n### 5. Display Item List\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/display_item_list.h`\\n**Class:** `DisplayItemList` (line 28)\\n\\nThe `DisplayItemList` is a container for a list of display items of various types. It records the sequence of paint operations generated during the paint walk. The `PaintController` maintains both the current and previous `DisplayItemList` to enable caching and invalidation logic. This list is eventually converted to compositor display operations via `PaintChunksToCcLayer`.\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\n1. **StyleResolver** computes styles → `ComputedStyle` objects\\n2. **LayoutObject** tree built from computed styles\\n3. **PaintLayer** tree created from select `LayoutObject` instances (stacking contexts)\\n4. **PaintController** traverses the `PaintLayer` tree during the paint phase\\n5. **DisplayItemList** accumulates paint operations\\n6. critical stages:\\n\\n### 1. Style Resolution\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/style_resolver.h`\\n**Class:** `StyleResolver` (line 63)\\n\\nThe `StyleResolver` class is the starting point of the rendering pipeline. It resolves computed styles for DOM elements based on the document's collection of stylesheets (user styles, author styles, UA styles). There is a 1-1 relationship between `StyleResolver` and `Document`. The `ResolveStyle` method produces a `ComputedStyle` for each element.\\n\\n### 2. Layout Tree Generation\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/layout_object.h`\\n**Class:** `LayoutObject` (line 270)\\n\\nThe `LayoutObject` class is the base class for the layout tree. It represents the layout abstraction of a DOM node. Layout objects are created based on the computed styles from `StyleResolver`. Each `LayoutObject` inherits from `GarbageCollected<LayoutObject>`, `ImageResourceObserver`, and `DisplayItemClient`, connecting the layout tree to the painting system.\\n\\n### 3. Painting Layer Hierarchy\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/paint_layer.h`\\n**Class:** `PaintLayer` (line 174)\\n\\nThe `PaintLayer` class represents the painting layer abstraction. Not all `LayoutObject` instances have a corresponding `PaintLayer`—only those that establish a stacking context or have special painting requirements. `PaintLayer` objects form a tree that determines the order and grouping of painting operations. Each `PaintLayer` maintains a reference to its associated `LayoutBoxModelObject`.\\n\\n### 4. Paint Controller and Display Item Processing\\n**File:** `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h`\\n**Class:** `PaintController` (line 131)\\n\\nThe `PaintController` is responsible for processing display items as they are produced during the painting traversal, and producing a final paint artifact when complete. It manages caching, cache invalidation, and merging of paint operations. During the paint walk, painters append display items to the `PaintController`'s display item list.\\n\\n### 5. It records the sequence of paint operations generated during the paint walk. The `PaintController` maintains both the current and previous `DisplayItemList` to enable caching and invalidation logic. Display items are converted to compositor paint chunks and eventually rasterized\\n\\nThis pipeline ensures efficient separation of concerns: style resolution handles CSS cascade, layout computes geometry, paint layers manage stacking and visibility, and the `PaintController`/`DisplayItemList` handle display list generation and caching.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
